`si_d~~h0_11_upa`


**1)** — *upa* abwehren, abhalten von (abl.): *vārddhakṣatrirupāsedhatpravaṇādiva kuñjaraḥ*
[MBH. 7,1748.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.1748) es ist wohl *˚kṣatrirapāsedhat — kuñjaram* zu lesen; vgl.
[7397.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.7397)

- **RU:** — *upa* отражать, удерживать от (abl.): *vārddhakṣatrirupāsedhatpravaṇādiva kuñjaraḥ*
[MBH. 7,1748.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.1748) вероятно, следует читать *˚kṣatrirapāsedhat — kuñjaram*; vgl.
[7397.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.7397)
- **EN:** — *upa* {to ward off, keep off from} (abl.): *vārddhakṣatrirupāsedhatpravaṇādiva kuñjaraḥ*
[MBH. 7,1748.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.1748) it should probably be read *˚kṣatrirapāsedhat — kuñjaram*; vgl.
[7397.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?7.7397)
  <sub>attested</sub>

## nis+sidh

`si_d~~h0_13_nis`


**1)** — *nis* verscheuchen: *niṣkravyādaṃ sedha*
[VS. 1,17.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/vajasasa/app1?1,17)
[ŚĀṄKH. ŚR. 16,18,20. fg.] Hierher *puruniḥṣidh* Vieles abwehrend.

- **RU:** — *nis* прогонять, распугивать: *niṣkravyādaṃ sedha*
[VS. 1,17.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/vajasasa/app1?1,17)
[ŚĀṄKH. ŚR. 16,18,20. fg.] Сюда же *puruniḥṣidh* отражающий многое, отгоняющий многих.
- **EN:** — *nis* {to scare away}: *niṣkravyādaṃ sedha*
[VS. 1,17.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/vajasasa/app1?1,17)
[ŚĀṄKH. ŚR. 16,18,20. fg.] Here belongs *puruniḥṣidh* {warding off much.}
  <sub>attested</sub>

## parā+sidh

`si_d~~h0_14_par_a`


**1)** — *parā* s. *parāsedha* in den Nachträgen.

- **RU:** — *parā* s. *parāsedha* в Nachträgen.

## pra+sidh

`si_d~~h0_16_pra`


**1)** — *pra* vorwärts treiben: *tābhyāṃ yuktvā prāsedhatsa udajayat*
[PAÑCAV. BR. 14,3,13.] *gāvau yuktau mo ṣu pra sedhīrmuhurinmamandhi* fahre nicht zu
[ṚV. 10,27,20.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv10.027.html#rv10.027.20) med.: *dhanuṣkeṇāniṣuṇā vrātyāḥ prasedhamānā yanti*
[LĀṬY. 8,6,8.]

- **RU:** — *pra* погонять вперёд, двигать вперёд: *tābhyāṃ yuktvā prāsedhatsa udajayat*
[PAÑCAV. BR. 14,3,13.] *gāvau yuktau mo ṣu pra sedhīrmuhurinmamandhi* не езди вперёд, не продолжай движения
[ṚV. 10,27,20.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv10.027.html#rv10.027.20) med.: *dhanuṣkeṇāniṣuṇā vrātyāḥ prasedhamānā yanti*
[LĀṬY. 8,6,8.]
- **EN:** — *pra* "to drive forward": *tābhyāṃ yuktvā prāsedhatsa udajayat*
[PAÑCAV. BR. 14,3,13.] *gāvau yuktau mo ṣu pra sedhīrmuhurinmamandhi* "do not drive on"
[ṚV. 10,27,20.](https://sanskrit-lexicon.github.io/rvlinks/rvhymns/rv10.027.html#rv10.027.20) med.: *dhanuṣkeṇāniṣuṇā vrātyāḥ prasedhamānā yanti*

## sidh

`si_d~~h0_zz_pw00`


**1.** √*sidh*¦, *sedhati* (*gatikarman*, *śāstre māṅgalye ca*)
- **EN:** **1.** √*sidh*¦, *sedhati* (*gatikarman*, *śāstre māṅgalye ca*)

**1)** — 1〉 scheuchen, treiben; vertreiben. *siddha* verscheucht.
- **EN:** — 1〉 to scare, drive; drive away. *siddha* scared away.

**2)** — 2〉 loben oder strafen [BHAṬṬ.]
- **EN:** — 2〉 to praise or punish [BHAṬṬ.]

**note1)** — *Desid. vom Caus. *siṣedhayiṣati*.
- **EN:** — *Desid. from Caus. *siṣedhayiṣati*.

**note2)** — *Intens. *seṣidhyate*. Vgl. *anu*.
- **EN:** — *Intens. *seṣidhyate*. Vgl. *anu*.

**prefix-1)** — Mit *anu* Intens. (*anuseṣidhat*) der Bahn entlang treiben, herleiten.

- **RU:** — С *anu* Intens. (*anuseṣidhat*) гнать по пути, вести.
- **EN:** — With *anu* Intens. (*anuseṣidhat*) to drive along the path, to derive.
  <sub>attested</sub>

**prefix-2-intro)** — Mit *apa*
- **EN:** — With *apa*

**prefix-2-1)** — 1〉 wegtreiben, verjagen.
- **EN:** — 1〉 to drive away, to chase off.

**prefix-2-2)** — 2〉 abwehren, abhalten, — von. (Abl.). v. l. auch Med.
- **EN:** — 2〉 to ward off, to keep from. (Abl.). v. l. also Med.

- **RU:** — С *abhi*, *˚ṣiddha* пригнанный сюда.
- **EN:** — With *abhi*, *˚ṣiddha* driven hither.

- **EN:** — 3〉 to ward off something [BHAṬṬ.]

## sidh

**2.** √*sidh*¦, *sidhyati* (metrisch oder ungenau auch Med.)
